  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_5bde2995-ac45-4623-b75d-c43002019c46'
      });
    }

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2591995763" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2591995763" />
    <a title="Cece Whittaker" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/70454422-cece-whittaker"><img alt="Cece Whittaker" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515012017p2/70454422.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2591995763?book_show_action=true">Nov 12, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cece Whittaker" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cece Whittaker" href="/user/show/70454422-cece-whittaker">Cece Whittaker</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2591995763" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9289229252309136355">Captivating Tale of Loss & Triumph in India, Oh Laxmi! by Catherine Forsayeth<br/>When I began reading this book, I was a little overwhelmed with the tragic misfortune, but I soon realized it was a tale told with good humor and a strong measure of wisdom. The characters are tapped and ultimately come alive with their quirks and strengths, interacting with such natural but intriguing and heartwarming behaviors. <br/>The maternal character, Mamta, issues a type of knowledge that is refreshingly realistic, a</span>
  <span id="freeText9289229252309136355" style="display:none">Captivating Tale of Loss &amp; Triumph in India, Oh Laxmi! by Catherine Forsayeth<br />When I began reading this book, I was a little overwhelmed with the tragic misfortune, but I soon realized it was a tale told with good humor and a strong measure of wisdom. The characters are tapped and ultimately come alive with their quirks and strengths, interacting with such natural but intriguing and heartwarming behaviors. <br />The maternal character, Mamta, issues a type of knowledge that is refreshingly realistic, and shares much of it with her daughters and husband, for example, “Enduring was one thing but making a cult of it was poisonous.” Ravi, her husband and the main character, brought such warmth and apparently uncommon appreciation of his wife that the reader falls in love with his strength and individuality, goatherd or not. <br />I think my favorite character, and in some ways the hero of the story, is the hospital doctor, who looks out for the relatively poor family and makes sure they receive good care, and then later, corrects a situation in which they were cheated. <br />As fortune starts to turn for Ravi’s family, he is treated in a Bombay hospital, by another good-natured doctor, a surgeon called Dr. Chitale. One of my favorite quotations, “Dr Chitale didn’t ask, seeing unusual things in India was the norm and having a goatherd change into an ATM dispensing cash in his hospital bed was just another one of those things,” give a good idea of the light-hearted and embracing narrative of Oh Laxmi by Catherine Forsayeth.<br /><br />I confess to getting a little lost with the names, as they are mostly unfamiliar to me as a Western reader, and I like to be able to pronounce the names, but that is not an author failing, just a need for broadening of the reader. While the presentation was patchy, with assorted mechanical issues, I can’t lower my rating from a 5 because the strength of the overall gift of the story was so great.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9289229252309136355" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2589913136" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2589913136" />
    <a title="Valery" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013735-valery"><img alt="Valery" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1480691033p2/4013735.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2589913136?book_show_action=true">Nov 10, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Valery" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Valery" href="/user/show/4013735-valery">Valery</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2589913136" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2722273255498488726">Oh Laxmi! by Catherine Forsayeth is a gem of a little book. We follow the seemingly simple life of Ravi, a goat herder who wants nothing more than a good life for his family. He has a lovely and devoted wife, and two daughters. Initially, the author gives a short overview of Ravi's earlier life as a young man and then on to his subsequent marriage. However, the main action of the story takes place as Ravi is having a typical day, herding his goats, when a series of most unseemly events befall hi</span>
  <span id="freeText2722273255498488726" style="display:none">Oh Laxmi! by Catherine Forsayeth is a gem of a little book. We follow the seemingly simple life of Ravi, a goat herder who wants nothing more than a good life for his family. He has a lovely and devoted wife, and two daughters. Initially, the author gives a short overview of Ravi's earlier life as a young man and then on to his subsequent marriage. However, the main action of the story takes place as Ravi is having a typical day, herding his goats, when a series of most unseemly events befall him. First he is injured when a giant seed pod hits him in his only good eye, and from there he is blinded. With the aid of a passerby he is taken to a hospital, but again, events just don't seem to go his way. This is a wondrous and inexplicable journey not only for Ravi, as he grows as a man and character, but for the reader as well. Forsayeth has created a beautiful and compelling world for the reader, as we learn Ravi's fate. Highly recommend for a treasure of a book. </span>
  <a data-text-id="2722273255498488726" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2610805041?book_show_action=true">Nov 30, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Profundito" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Profundito" href="/user/show/84279706-profundito">Profundito</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2610805041" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2704016595542311148">The writing isn’t without flaw, but it’s well worth the read.<br/><br/>The story follows Ravi and his family during his constant venture to provide and stay strong. Tragedy soon strikes and Ravi is thrown into a series of circumstances that he works to make the best of. Each character is described well, and has their own unique personas that lend themselves well to the story. Forsayeth does a good job of tying in the characters to tragedy, and making them believable despite circumstances that would hinder</span>
  <span id="freeText2704016595542311148" style="display:none">The writing isn’t without flaw, but it’s well worth the read.<br /><br />The story follows Ravi and his family during his constant venture to provide and stay strong. Tragedy soon strikes and Ravi is thrown into a series of circumstances that he works to make the best of. Each character is described well, and has their own unique personas that lend themselves well to the story. Forsayeth does a good job of tying in the characters to tragedy, and making them believable despite circumstances that would hinder most. Finding the best in bad situations, and being happy with what life gives you is a major part of this story. There are some pretty great lines in the text, as well, that really show off Forsayeth’s creativity with writing.<br /><br />The story is definitely worth your time, and it wont waste what you’ve given it.<br /></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2585605720" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6208340827236963118">Ravi isn't the richest man, or the most fortunate (he is blind in one eye after all), but he has found a great deal of contentment in his life. His work as a goat farmer is going well, his two daughters are set for university and marriage, and he has genuine love for his wife, he was arranged to wed many years before. That is until one day, a seemingly innocuous event changes everything. A giant seed pod of the Moringa tree hits him in his good eye. His screams of pain and the unfortunate passin</span>
  <span id="freeText6208340827236963118" style="display:none">Ravi isn't the richest man, or the most fortunate (he is blind in one eye after all), but he has found a great deal of contentment in his life. His work as a goat farmer is going well, his two daughters are set for university and marriage, and he has genuine love for his wife, he was arranged to wed many years before. That is until one day, a seemingly innocuous event changes everything. A giant seed pod of the Moringa tree hits him in his good eye. His screams of pain and the unfortunate passing of a motorbike cause his goats to scatter and flee. The man on the motorbike comes to his aid, and they set off for help, but Ravi's bad luck is not over yet. What will the future hold for his family?<br /><br />'Oh Laxmi!' by Catherine Forsayeth is wonderfully descriptive, you do become engrossed with the world she has created. I felt a part of the journey that Ravi takes, both literally and in his own development. I love this book and would recommend it to all fans of contemporary fiction.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6208340827236963118" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('itDywuzjAgt3+Z11mqdMKAoXhS77tteTOfIQza14n5bMAxFRV1V0INhzRTwvIsIkanpRR8gqMqRFTYswi+Y2yw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('edNH1BlNYVu78mCfF1tuwZsr7HoDMBIBrOt8ILCSV+g/AKRHovsXcBR4uNai3uDN+0Y4EzCs9zbQVOfdlgz+tQ==')})
  }

      var newTip = new Tip($('bookCover_36334989'), "\n\n  <h2><a class=\"readable bookTitle\" href=\"https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/36334989-the-influence-of-military-strategies-to-business?from_choice=false&amp;from_home_module=false\">The Influence of Military Strategies to Business<\/a><\/h2>\n\n      <div>\n        by <a class=\"authorName\" href=\"/author/show/5692437.M_D_White?a=9&amp;origin=related_works\">M.D. White<\/a><span title=\"Goodreads Author!\">*<\/span>\n      <\/div>\n\n          <div class=\"smallText uitext darkGreyText\">\n            <span class=\"minirating\"><span class=\"stars staticStars notranslate\"><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p3\"><\/span><\/span> 4.08 avg rating &mdash; 498 ratings<\/span>            &mdash; published \n          <\/div>\n\n    <div class=\"addBookTipDescription\">\n      \n<span id=\"freeTextContainer1082070524140169311\">Business Management and Leadership Expert, M.D. White, releases new book, “The Influence of Military Strategies to Business.” A military-based guide to business takes the best wartime tactics and practices and teaches you how you can apply them in yo<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText1082070524140169311\" style=\"display:none\">Business Management and Leadership Expert, M.D. White, releases new book, “The Influence of Military Strategies to Business.” A military-based guide to business takes the best wartime tactics and practices and teaches you how you can apply them in your business—and your political or personal life—successfully. The book is scheduled for release on the 1st of October. As a Business Strategy and Psychological Warfare Consultant, M.D. White wrote this book utilizing his countless experiences over the years to properly proffer working, tested and trusted strategies to help business owners or employees, business managers or executives, politicians and or public figures manage high-stake business and leadership situations with the greatest success. White had this to say: &quot;No amount of experience in crucial conversations, or business negotiations, can prepare you better than the information you\'ll gleam from this manual. It\'s truly a politician’s guide to psychological warfare. Perhaps its President Trumps bible, and what he reads everynight. The moral of the story is: Use it, or be used by it! Current geopolitical controversies only emphasize this point.&quot; Many have deliberated over the effect of military strategies in business, but M.D. White cuts to the chase and reveals the raw and missing pieces all other military strategy discussions have left out. In this book, White extracts the key ingredients of military strategies and the applications which are left out in most discussions. For the first time ever there is a clear work-around of military strategies and an easy to understand roadmap on learning how to unlock, grow and strengthen from within one’s influence, presence and abilities. The Author further stressed the effectiveness of military strategies in business. “This military-based guide to business takes the best wartime tactics and practices and teaches you how you can apply them in your business—and your political or personal life—successfully. Developed within a systematic and comprehensive framework, this book utilizes the art of war in a whole new way and reveals that the path to a smooth business victory and mutually beneficial dialogue can be found in an unexpected but rewarding place.”  The world of business is a battlefield. You must be prepared.  Sun Tzu said, “The art of war teaches us to rely not on the likelihood of the enemy’s not coming, but on our own readiness to receive him.” The takeaway? Do everything in your power to be prepared, because it\'s only a matter of time before something goes wrong. If you are running, founding, working in any business, or are in an environment where ‘politics’ yield to nobody, The Influence of Military Strategies to Business is the preparation you need to succeed.  This military-based guide to business takes the best wartime tactics and practices and teaches you how you can apply them in your business—and your personal life—successfully. With its systematic and comprehensive framework, this book utilizes the art of war in a whole new way and reveals that the path to a smooth business victory can be found in an unexpected but rewarding
